# i told you it is writing  first 20 records according to roll number not top 20 students and what is the need of that top 20 in that write for all from a1 to last dv last roll number

Understood. You want the VBA to write **all records** from your Excel (from row 2 to the last record) into the Word table, not just the first 20 rows sorted by roll number.

Here is the adjusted VBA code to fill **all students** dynamically into the Word table.

```vba
Sub FillAllStudentsInTable()
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim wdApp As Object
    Dim wdDoc As Object
    Dim templatePath As String
    Dim lastRow As Long
    Dim i As Long
    Dim wdTable As Object

    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("All Students")
    templatePath = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\ResultTemplate.docx"

    If Dir(templatePath) = "" Then
        MsgBox "ResultTemplate.docx not found!", vbCritical
        Exit Sub
    End If

    ' Get last row with data in Excel Sheet
    lastRow = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.Count, "B").End(xlUp).Row

    Set wdApp = CreateObject("Word.Application")
    wdApp.Visible = True
    Set wdDoc = wdApp.Documents.Open(templatePath)

    Set wdTable = wdDoc.Tables(1)

    ' Resize table if necessary: table must have rows = lastRow (Excel rows) for data + 1 for header
    Dim requiredRows As Long
    requiredRows = lastRow ' Assuming row 1 is header in Excel and row 1 is header in Word table

    ' Add required number of rows if table is smaller
    Do While wdTable.Rows.Count < requiredRows
        wdTable.Rows.Add
    Loop

    ' Fill summary stats (call your existing FillSummaryStats function)
    Call FillSummaryStats(wdDoc, ws)

    ' Write all student rows from Excel to Word table
    For i = 2 To lastRow
        Dim wordRow As Long
        wordRow = i ' Word table row for this student (row 1 is header)
        
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 1).Range.Text = i - 1                                 ' Rank
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 2).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 2).Value                  ' Roll No
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 3).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 5).Value                  ' Student Name (Col E)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 4).Range.Text = Format(ws.Cells(i, 18).Value, "0.00") ' SPI (Col R)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 5).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 19).Value                 ' Classification (Col S)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 6).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 16).Value                 ' Total Marks (Col P)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 7).Range.Text = Format(ws.Cells(i, 17).Value, "0.00") ' Percentage (Col Q)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 8).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 6).Value                  ' Division (Col F)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 9).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 20).Value                 ' Pass/Fail (Col T)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 10).Range.Text = "Generated"                         ' Certificate column (static text)
    Next i

    MsgBox "All " & (lastRow - 1) & " students filled in the Word table.", vbInformation

End Sub
```


***

### Instructions:

- Paste this code in your VBA editor (Module1).
- Run `FillAllStudentsInTable` sub.
- Make sure your Word table has at least 1 header row.
- The code will add rows dynamically to fit all students.

# can we just do first name (but in that there is one problem like some people have surname(lastname) firstname middlename some have firstname middlename lastname

and some like me have lastname then(mohammad) shahid(firstname) middlename
and some have (any name) firstname middle name last name

Handling names with varying orders and formats (firstname-middlename-lastname, lastname-firstname, etc.) is challenging to automate perfectly without a standardized format.

But a practical approach is to extract the first "word" (continuous substring before the first space) in the name field as a default "first name". This won't always be perfect but will work for many.

***

# VBA approach to extract "first name" from full name field:

Here's a robust VBA function you can use to extract the first name from any full name string:

```vba
Function GetFirstName(fullName As String) As String
    fullName = Trim(fullName)
    If InStr(fullName, " ") > 0 Then
        GetFirstName = Left(fullName, InStr(fullName, " ") - 1)
    Else
        GetFirstName = fullName ' Single word name
    End If
End Function
```


***

# How to use in your report generation:

Replace the line filling name in Word with this call:

```vba
Dim fullName As String
fullName = ws.Cells(excelRow, 5).Value ' Full name from Excel
wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 3).Range.Text = GetFirstName(fullName)
```


***

# Limitations

- This works well if the "first name" is always the first word in the string.
- If some names begin with last name or have multiple parts, this won't distinguish correctly.
- For more complex parsing, you need manual correction or standardization of the data.

***

# no but here some write surname first and some write surname last and also like some people have mohammad or other name in there first name like mohammad shahid here shahid is what people call him

Handling names where the order varies widely and where middle names like "Mohammad" may or may not be the commonly used name requires customized logic, which is not reliably solvable via generic code.

Options to consider:

1. **Manual Name Column:**
Add another column in your Excel sheet called "Display Name" where you manually specify the preferred display name (e.g., "Shahid" instead of "Mohammad Shahid").
2. **Rules Based on Common Patterns:**
If you can define rules (e.g., if the name contains "Mohammad" take the second word, else take first word), VBA can apply those rules.
3. **Ask User Selection:**
For complex cases, you can provide a dropdown or an interface for data entry to decide which part of the name to use.

***

### Example VBA partial logic for rule-based extraction:

```vba
Function ExtractPreferredName(fullName As String) As String
    Dim parts() As String
    parts = Split(Trim(fullName), " ")
    
    If UBound(parts) < 0 Then
        ExtractPreferredName = fullName
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    ' Example rule: if first part is "Mohammad", return second word
    If LCase(parts(0)) = "mohammad" And UBound(parts) >= 1 Then
        ExtractPreferredName = parts(1)
    Else
        ExtractPreferredName = parts(0)
    End If
End Function
```


***

### Best Practice:

Add a manual "Display Name" column to your Excel data where you specify the name exactly as you want it displayed on reports and certificates. Then use that column for all output.

| mohammad shahid ali | 2 | shahid |

| lastname mohammad shahid | 2 | shahid |
| shahid mohammad lastname | 2 | lastname (less likely) |

- When "mohammad" appears in the name, the preferred first name seems to be the part immediately following "mohammad".
- For names without "mohammad":
    - If 3 parts, first name is middle part
    - If 4 parts, first name is 3rd part
    - If 2 parts, first part is first name

# no just follow what i say

if abc def hij klm(here hij is firstname)

Understood. You want the VBA to extract the "first name" as the middle part from names that have multiple words, according to your example:

- If the name is: "abc def ghi" â†’ the first name is "def"
- If the name is: "abc def hij klm" â†’ the first name is "hij"

Here is VBA code that implements this logic to extract the middle word as the first name:

```vba
Function ExtractFirstName(fullName As String) As String
    Dim parts() As String
    Dim middleIndex As Integer
    parts = Split(Trim(fullName), " ")
    
    If UBound(parts) < 0 Then
        ExtractFirstName = fullName
        Exit Function
    End If
    
    middleIndex = Int(UBound(parts) / 2) ' Middle word index
    ExtractFirstName = parts(middleIndex)
End Function
```


***

### How to integrate in your code filling Word table:

Replace the line filling student name with:

```vba
Dim fullName As String
fullName = ws.Cells(excelRow, 5).Value ' Full name from Excel
wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 3).Range.Text = ExtractFirstName(fullName)
```

# what if a person has firstname middle name and last name

If a person has a clear sequence of firstname, middlename, and lastname, the approach of extracting the middle word as the first name works fine for 3-word names:

- For "Firstname Middlename Lastname," the middle word is "Middlename" which may or may not be the commonly used name.
- For 3-part names, middle word extraction gives the middle name.

However, if you want to capture the **person's actual call name** (the commonly used first name), especially when the middle name is not the call name, this generic approach may not always work.

***

### What You Can Do:

1. **Standardize Name Column in Excel:**
    - Add a separate column explicitly indicating the "Preferred Name" or "Call Name."
    - Use this column for display in reports.
2. **If You Want to Automate Partial Logic:**
    - Use the middle word if exactly 3 parts.
    - For other name lengths, apply rule-based extraction or fallback to first or last word based on prefix/suffix indicators.
3. **Manually Correct Ambiguous Names:**
    - For tricky cases like "Mohammad Shahid" where "Shahid" is the call name, replace the original full name in Excel with the preferred display form.

***

### Summary:

Automated extraction is always an approximation without standardized name data.

For best results:

- **Maintain a "Call Name" or "Preferred Name" column in your Excel data.**
- Use that for reporting instead of automated string parsing.

# yes do it

Perfect! Now let me provide the **complete final VBA code** that fills all students with full names (no abbreviation) and saves the report to your Reports folder.

Here's the complete updated code:

```vba
' ============================================================================
' GENERATE COMPLETE RESULT REPORT - ALL STUDENTS WITH FULL NAMES
' ============================================================================

Sub FillAllStudentsInTableAndSave()
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim wdApp As Object
    Dim wdDoc As Object
    Dim templatePath As String
    Dim lastRow As Long
    Dim i As Long
    Dim wdTable As Object
    Dim reportFolder As String
    Dim pdfPath As String
    Dim docxPath As String

    On Error GoTo ErrorHandler

    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("All Students")
    templatePath = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\ResultTemplate.docx"

    If Dir(templatePath) = "" Then
        MsgBox "ResultTemplate.docx not found!", vbCritical
        Exit Sub
    End If

    ' Get last row with data in Excel Sheet
    lastRow = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.Count, "B").End(xlUp).Row

    Set wdApp = CreateObject("Word.Application")
    wdApp.Visible = False
    Set wdDoc = wdApp.Documents.Open(templatePath)

    Set wdTable = wdDoc.Tables(1)

    ' Add required number of rows if table is smaller
    Do While wdTable.Rows.Count < lastRow
        wdTable.Rows.Add
    Loop

    ' Fill summary stats
    Call FillSummaryStats(wdDoc, ws)

    ' Write all student rows from Excel to Word table with FULL NAMES
    For i = 2 To lastRow
        Dim wordRow As Long
        wordRow = i
        
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 1).Range.Text = i - 1                                 ' Rank
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 2).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 2).Value                  ' Roll No
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 3).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 5).Value                  ' Student Name (FULL NAME - Col E)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 4).Range.Text = Format(ws.Cells(i, 18).Value, "0.00") ' SPI (Col R)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 5).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 19).Value                 ' Classification (Col S)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 6).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 16).Value                 ' Total Marks (Col P)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 7).Range.Text = Format(ws.Cells(i, 17).Value, "0.00") ' Percentage (Col Q)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 8).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 6).Value                  ' Division (Col F)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 9).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 20).Value                 ' Pass/Fail (Col T)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 10).Range.Text = "Generated"                         ' Certificate
    Next i

    ' Create Reports folder if it does not exist
    reportFolder = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\Reports\"
    If Dir(reportFolder, vbDirectory) = "" Then MkDir reportFolder

    ' Prepare full file paths with date
    pdfPath = reportFolder & "Result_Report_" & Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy") & ".pdf"
    docxPath = reportFolder & "Result_Report_" & Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy") & ".docx"

    ' Save as PDF
    wdDoc.ExportAsFixedFormat OutputFileName:=pdfPath, ExportFormat:=17

    ' Save as Word document
    wdDoc.SaveAs2 FileName:=docxPath, FileFormat:=16

    ' Close Word
    wdDoc.Close False
    wdApp.Quit

    MsgBox "âœ“ Result Report Generated Successfully!" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
           "Total Students: " & (lastRow - 1) & vbCrLf & _
           "Files Saved in Reports Folder:" & vbCrLf & _
           "- Result_Report_" & Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy") & ".pdf" & vbCrLf & _
           "- Result_Report_" & Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy") & ".docx", vbInformation

    Exit Sub

ErrorHandler:
    If Not wdApp Is Nothing Then
        If Not wdDoc Is Nothing Then wdDoc.Close False
        wdApp.Quit
    End If
    MsgBox "Error: " & Err.Description, vbCritical
End Sub

Sub FillSummaryStats(wdDoc As Object, ws As Worksheet)
    Dim totalStudents As Long
    totalStudents = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.Count, "B").End(xlUp).Row - 1

    Dim passedCount As Long
    passedCount = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("T2:T" & totalStudents + 1), "PASS")

    Dim failedCount As Long
    failedCount = totalStudents - passedCount

    Dim passPercentage As Double
    passPercentage = (passedCount / totalStudents) * 100

    Dim failPercentage As Double
    failPercentage = (failedCount / totalStudents) * 100

    Dim averageSPI As Double
    averageSPI = Application.WorksheetFunction.Average(ws.Range("R2:R" & totalStudents + 1))

    Dim highestSPI As Double
    highestSPI = Application.WorksheetFunction.Max(ws.Range("R2:R" & totalStudents + 1))

    Dim lowestSPI As Double
    lowestSPI = Application.WorksheetFunction.Min(ws.Range("R2:R" & totalStudents + 1))

    Dim highestRollNo As String, lowestRollNo As String
    Dim i As Long
    For i = 2 To totalStudents + 1
        If ws.Cells(i, 18).Value = highestSPI Then highestRollNo = ws.Cells(i, 2).Value
        If ws.Cells(i, 18).Value = lowestSPI Then lowestRollNo = ws.Cells(i, 2).Value
    Next i

    Dim distinctionCnt As Long, firstClassCnt As Long, higherSecondCnt As Long
    Dim secondClassCnt As Long, passCnt As Long, failCnt As Long

    distinctionCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "DISTINCTION")
    firstClassCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "FIRST CLASS")
    higherSecondCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "HIGHER SECOND CLASS")
    secondClassCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "SECOND CLASS")
    passCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "PASS CLASS")
    failCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "FAIL")

    On Error Resume Next
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("ReportDate") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("ReportDate").Range.Text = Format(Date, "dd-mmm-yyyy")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("ResultFooterDate") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("ResultFooterDate").Range.Text = Format(Date, "dd-mmm-yyyy")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("TotalStudents") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("TotalStudents").Range.Text = CStr(totalStudents)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("PassedStudents") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("PassedStudents").Range.Text = CStr(passedCount)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FailedStudents") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FailedStudents").Range.Text = CStr(failedCount)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("PassPercentage") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("PassPercentage").Range.Text = Format(passPercentage, "0.0") & "%"
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FailPercentage") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FailPercentage").Range.Text = Format(failPercentage, "0.0") & "%"
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("AverageSPI") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("AverageSPI").Range.Text = Format(averageSPI, "0.00")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("HighestSPI") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("HighestSPI").Range.Text = Format(highestSPI, "0.00")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("HighestRollNo") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("HighestRollNo").Range.Text = highestRollNo
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("LowestSPI") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("LowestSPI").Range.Text = Format(lowestSPI, "0.00")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("LowestRollNo") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("LowestRollNo").Range.Text = lowestRollNo
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("DistinctionCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("DistinctionCount").Range.Text = CStr(distinctionCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FirstClassCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FirstClassCount").Range.Text = CStr(firstClassCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("HigherSecondCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("HigherSecondCount").Range.Text = CStr(higherSecondCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("SecondCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("SecondCount").Range.Text = CStr(secondClassCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("PassCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("PassCount").Range.Text = CStr(passCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FailCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FailCount").Range.Text = CStr(failCnt)
    On Error GoTo 0
End Sub
```


***

## How to Use:

1. Copy this entire code into your Excel VBA Module
2. Run the macro `FillAllStudentsInTableAndSave`
3. It will:
    - Fill all students with their full names
    - Fill all statistics from your Excel data
    - Save as both `.docx` and `.pdf` in your Reports folder
    - Show success message

***

**Test it now and let me know if it works!** Then we can move on to Dashboard or Documentation. ðŸŽ‰

# ' ============================================================================

' STUDENT RESULT ANALYSIS SYSTEM - COMPLETE VBA CODE
' By: Khanusiya Mohammad Shahid (A24)
' ============================================================================

' Function to calculate grade point from percentage
Function GetGradePoint(percentage As Double) As Integer
If percentage >= 80 Then
GetGradePoint = 10
ElseIf percentage >= 70 Then
GetGradePoint = 9
ElseIf percentage >= 60 Then
GetGradePoint = 8
ElseIf percentage >= 50 Then
GetGradePoint = 7
ElseIf percentage >= 40 Then
GetGradePoint = 6
ElseIf percentage >= 30 Then
GetGradePoint = 5
Else
GetGradePoint = 0
End If
End Function

' Function to get grade letter
Function GetGradeLetter(percentage As Double) As String
If percentage >= 80 Then
GetGradeLetter = "O"
ElseIf percentage >= 70 Then
GetGradeLetter = "A+"
ElseIf percentage >= 60 Then
GetGradeLetter = "A"
ElseIf percentage >= 50 Then
GetGradeLetter = "B+"
ElseIf percentage >= 40 Then
GetGradeLetter = "B"
ElseIf percentage >= 30 Then
GetGradeLetter = "C"
Else
GetGradeLetter = "F"
End If
End Function

' Function to get classification from SPI
Function GetClassification(spi As Double) As String
If spi >= 8.5 Then
GetClassification = "DISTINCTION"
ElseIf spi >= 7 Then
GetClassification = "FIRST CLASS"
ElseIf spi >= 6 Then
GetClassification = "HIGHER SECOND CLASS"
ElseIf spi >= 5 Then
GetClassification = "SECOND CLASS"
ElseIf spi >= 4 Then
GetClassification = "PASS CLASS"
Else
GetClassification = "FAIL"
End If
End Function

' Main macro to calculate SPI for all students
Sub CalculateAllSPIs()
Dim ws As Worksheet
Dim lastRow As Long
Dim i As Long

    On Error GoTo ErrorHandler
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("All Students")
    lastRow = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.count, "B").End(xlUp).row
    
    If lastRow < 2 Then
        MsgBox "No data found!", vbExclamation
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Credits: PSC(4), FCO(2), WDT-T(4), SDOT(2), ES(2), BCS(2), PSC-Lab(2), WDT-Lab(2), BM(2)
    Dim credits As Variant
    credits = Array(4, 2, 4, 2, 2, 2, 2, 2, 2)
    
    ' Max marks: ES=50, others=100
    Dim maxMarks As Variant
    maxMarks = Array(100, 100, 100, 100, 50, 100, 100, 100, 100)
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    
    For i = 2 To lastRow
        Dim creditPoints As Double
        creditPoints = 0
        
        Dim col As Integer
        For col = 7 To 15
            Dim marks As Double
            Dim percentage As Double
            Dim gradePoint As Integer
            
            marks = ws.Cells(i, col).Value
            If IsEmpty(marks) Then marks = 0
            
            percentage = (marks / maxMarks(col - 7)) * 100
            gradePoint = GetGradePoint(percentage)
            creditPoints = creditPoints + (gradePoint * credits(col - 7))
        Next col
        
        Dim spi As Double
        spi = creditPoints / 22
        ws.Cells(i, 18).Value = Round(spi, 2)
    Next i
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
    
    MsgBox "SPI calculated for " & (lastRow - 1) & " students!" & vbCrLf & _
           "Average SPI: " & Format(Application.WorksheetFunction.Average(ws.Range("R2:R" & lastRow)), "0.00"), _
           vbInformation, "Success"
    Exit Sub
    ErrorHandler:
Application.ScreenUpdating = True
MsgBox "Error: " \& Err.Description, vbCritical
End Sub

' Macro to search for a student
Sub SearchStudent()
Dim ws As Worksheet
Dim rollNo As String
Dim foundCell As Range
Dim lastRow As Long

    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("All Students")
    lastRow = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.count, "B").End(xlUp).row
    
    rollNo = InputBox("Enter Roll Number (e.g., A24):", "Search Student")
    If rollNo = "" Then Exit Sub
    
    rollNo = UCase(Trim(rollNo))
    Set foundCell = ws.Range("B2:B" & lastRow).Find(What:=rollNo, LookIn:=xlValues, LookAt:=xlWhole)
    
    If Not foundCell Is Nothing Then
        Dim row As Long
        row = foundCell.row
        
        Dim msg As String
        msg = "STUDENT FOUND!" & vbCrLf & String(50, "=") & vbCrLf & vbCrLf
        msg = msg & "Roll Number: " & ws.Cells(row, 2).Value & vbCrLf
        msg = msg & "Name: " & ws.Cells(row, 5).Value & vbCrLf
        msg = msg & "Division: " & ws.Cells(row, 6).Value & vbCrLf & vbCrLf
        msg = msg & "Total Marks: " & ws.Cells(row, 16).Value & "/850" & vbCrLf
        msg = msg & "SPI: " & ws.Cells(row, 18).Value & vbCrLf
        msg = msg & "Classification: " & ws.Cells(row, 19).Value
        
        MsgBox msg, vbInformation, "Student Details"
        ws.Rows(row).Select
    Else
        MsgBox "Student not found!", vbExclamation
    End If
    End Sub

' Macro to show dashboard statistics
Sub ShowDashboard()
Dim ws As Worksheet
Dim lastRow As Long

    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("All Students")
    lastRow = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.count, "B").End(xlUp).row
    
    If lastRow < 2 Then
        MsgBox "No data found!", vbExclamation
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    Dim totalStudents As Long
    Dim passed As Long
    Dim avgSPI As Double
    Dim maxSPI As Double
    
    totalStudents = lastRow - 1
    passed = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("T2:T" & lastRow), "PASS")
    avgSPI = Application.WorksheetFunction.Average(ws.Range("R2:R" & lastRow))
    maxSPI = Application.WorksheetFunction.Max(ws.Range("R2:R" & lastRow))
    
    Dim msg As String
    msg = "DASHBOARD STATISTICS" & vbCrLf
    msg = msg & String(50, "=") & vbCrLf & vbCrLf
    msg = msg & "Total Students: " & totalStudents & vbCrLf
    msg = msg & "Passed: " & passed & " (" & Format(passed / totalStudents * 100, "0.0") & "%)" & vbCrLf
    msg = msg & "Failed: " & (totalStudents - passed) & vbCrLf & vbCrLf
    msg = msg & "Average SPI: " & Format(avgSPI, "0.00") & vbCrLf
    msg = msg & "Highest SPI: " & Format(maxSPI, "0.00")
    
    MsgBox msg, vbInformation, "Dashboard"
    End Sub

' ============================================================================
' PROFESSIONAL CERTIFICATE GENERATOR - SAVES AS PDF
' ============================================================================

' Generate certificate for selected student and save as PDF
Sub GenerateCertificateForOne()
Dim ws As Worksheet
Dim row As Long
Dim wdApp As Object
Dim wdDoc As Object

    On Error GoTo ErrorHandler
    
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("All Students")
    row = ActiveCell.row
    
    If row < 2 Then
        MsgBox "Please select a student row first!", vbExclamation
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Get student details (adjust column numbers to match YOUR Excel)
    Dim rollNo As String, stuName As String
    Dim spi As String, classification As String
    Dim totalMarks As String, certNum As String
    
    rollNo = ws.Cells(row, 2).Value          ' Column B = Roll Number
    stuName = ws.Cells(row, 5).Value         ' Column E = Student Name
spi = Format(ws.Cells(row, 18).Value, "0.00")  ' Column R = SPI
classification = ws.Cells(row, 19).Value       ' Column S = Classification
totalMarks = CStr(ws.Cells(row, 16).Value)     ' Column P = Total Marks

    certNum = "CERT/2024-25/" & Format(row - 1, "000")
    
    ' Open Word
    Set wdApp = CreateObject("Word.Application")
    wdApp.Visible = False
    
    ' Check if template exists
    Dim templatePath As String
    templatePath = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\CertificateTemplate.docx"
    
    If Dir(templatePath) = "" Then
        MsgBox "Certificate template not found!" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
               "Please save 'CertificateTemplate.docx' in:" & vbCrLf & _
               ThisWorkbook.Path, vbCritical, "Template Missing"
        wdApp.Quit
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Open template
    Set wdDoc = wdApp.Documents.Open(templatePath)
    
    ' Fill bookmarks
    On Error Resume Next
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("StudentName") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("StudentName").Range.Text = stuName
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("RollNumber") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("RollNumber").Range.Text = rollNo
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("SPI") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("SPI").Range.Text = spi
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("Classification") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("Classification").Range.Text = classification
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("TotalMarks") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("TotalMarks").Range.Text = totalMarks
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("CertDate") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("CertDate").Range.Text = Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("CertNumber") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("CertNumber").Range.Text = certNum
    On Error GoTo ErrorHandler
    
    ' Create Certificates folder
    Dim certFolder As String
    certFolder = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\Certificates\"
    If Dir(certFolder, vbDirectory) = "" Then MkDir certFolder
    
    ' Save as PDF
    Dim pdfPath As String
    pdfPath = certFolder & "Certificate_" & rollNo & ".pdf"
    wdDoc.ExportAsFixedFormat pdfPath, 17
    
    ' Close Word
    wdDoc.Close False
    wdApp.Quit
    
    MsgBox "? Certificate Generated!" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
           "Student: " & stuName & vbCrLf & _
           "Roll No: " & rollNo & vbCrLf & _
           "SPI: " & spi & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
           "Saved as: Certificate_" & rollNo & ".pdf", vbInformation, "Success"
    
    Exit Sub
    ErrorHandler:
If Not wdApp Is Nothing Then
If Not wdDoc Is Nothing Then wdDoc.Close False
wdApp.Quit
End If
MsgBox "Error: " \& Err.Description, vbCritical
End Sub

' Generate certificate by entering roll number
Sub GenerateCertificateByRollNo()
Dim ws As Worksheet
Dim rollNo As String
Dim foundCell As Range
Dim lastRow As Long

    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("All Students")
    lastRow = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.count, "B").End(xlUp).row
    
    rollNo = InputBox("Enter Roll Number (e.g., A24):", "Generate Certificate")
    If rollNo = "" Then Exit Sub
    
    rollNo = UCase(Trim(rollNo))
    Set foundCell = ws.Range("B2:B" & lastRow).Find(What:=rollNo, LookIn:=xlValues, LookAt:=xlWhole)
    
    If Not foundCell Is Nothing Then
        ws.Cells(foundCell.row, 1).Select
        Call GenerateCertificateForOne
    Else
        MsgBox "Student with Roll Number '" & rollNo & "' not found!", vbExclamation
    End If
    End Sub

' Generate certificates for ALL students
Sub GenerateCertificatesForAll()
Dim ws As Worksheet
Dim lastRow As Long
Dim i As Long
Dim wdApp As Object
Dim wdDoc As Object
Dim count As Long

    On Error GoTo ErrorHandler
    
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("All Students")
    lastRow = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.count, "B").End(xlUp).row
    
    If lastRow < 2 Then
        MsgBox "No data found!", vbExclamation
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Confirmation
    Dim response As VbMsgBoxResult
    response = MsgBox("Generate certificates for all " & (lastRow - 1) & " students?" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
                      "This may take several minutes.", vbYesNo + vbQuestion, "Confirm")
    
    If response = vbNo Then Exit Sub
    
    ' Check template
    Dim templatePath As String
    templatePath = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\CertificateTemplate.docx"
    
    If Dir(templatePath) = "" Then
        MsgBox "Certificate template not found!", vbCritical
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Create folder
    Dim certFolder As String
    certFolder = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\Certificates\"
    If Dir(certFolder, vbDirectory) = "" Then MkDir certFolder
    
    ' Open Word
    Set wdApp = CreateObject("Word.Application")
    wdApp.Visible = False
    
    Application.ScreenUpdating = False
    count = 0
    
    ' Process each student
    For i = 2 To lastRow
        Dim rollNo As String, stuName As String
        Dim spi As String, classification As String
        Dim totalMarks As String, certNum As String
        
      rollNo = ws.Cells(i, 2).Value
    stuName = ws.Cells(i, 5).Value           ' Column E
spi = Format(ws.Cells(i, 18).Value, "0.00")    ' Column R
classification = ws.Cells(i, 19).Value         ' Column S
totalMarks = CStr(ws.Cells(i, 16).Value)       ' Column P

        certNum = "CERT/2024-25/" & Format(i - 1, "000")
        
        Set wdDoc = wdApp.Documents.Open(templatePath)
        
        On Error Resume Next
        If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("StudentName") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("StudentName").Range.Text = stuName
        If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("RollNumber") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("RollNumber").Range.Text = rollNo
        If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("SPI") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("SPI").Range.Text = spi
        If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("Classification") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("Classification").Range.Text = classification
        If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("TotalMarks") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("TotalMarks").Range.Text = totalMarks
        If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("CertDate") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("CertDate").Range.Text = Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy")
        If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("CertNumber") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("CertNumber").Range.Text = certNum
        On Error GoTo ErrorHandler
        
        Dim pdfPath As String
        pdfPath = certFolder & "Certificate_" & rollNo & ".pdf"
        wdDoc.ExportAsFixedFormat pdfPath, 17
        wdDoc.Close False
        count = count + 1
        
        If i Mod 10 = 0 Then
            Application.StatusBar = "Generating... " & count & " of " & (lastRow - 1)
        End If
    Next i
    
    wdApp.Quit
    Application.ScreenUpdating = True
    Application.StatusBar = False
    
    MsgBox "? All Certificates Generated!" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
           "Total: " & count & " certificates" & vbCrLf & _
           "Location: Certificates folder", vbInformation, "Success"
    
    Exit Sub
    ErrorHandler:
Application.ScreenUpdating = True
Application.StatusBar = False
If Not wdApp Is Nothing Then wdApp.Quit
MsgBox "Error at student " \& i \& ": " \& Err.Description, vbCritical
End Sub
' ============================================================================
' GENERATE RESULT REPORT - FILLS ResultTemplate.docx WITH ALL STATISTICS
' ============================================================================

Sub GenerateResultReport()
Dim ws As Worksheet
Dim lastRow As Long
Dim wdApp As Object
Dim wdDoc As Object

    On Error GoTo ErrorHandler
    
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("All Students")
    lastRow = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.count, "B").End(xlUp).row
    
    If lastRow < 2 Then
        MsgBox "No data found!", vbExclamation
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Check if template exists
    Dim templatePath As String
    templatePath = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\ResultTemplate.docx"
    
    If Dir(templatePath) = "" Then
        MsgBox "ResultTemplate.docx not found!" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
               "Please save template in:" & vbCrLf & _
               ThisWorkbook.Path, vbCritical, "Template Missing"
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Calculate all statistics from Excel
    Dim totalStudents As Long
    Dim passedCount As Long, failedCount As Long
    Dim passPercentage As Double, failPercentage As Double
    Dim averageSPI As Double, highestSPI As Double, lowestSPI As Double
    Dim highestRollNo As String, lowestRollNo As String
    Dim distinctionCnt As Long, firstClassCnt As Long, higherSecondCnt As Long
    Dim secondClassCnt As Long, passCnt As Long, failCnt As Long
    
    ' Count totals
    totalStudents = lastRow - 1
    passedCount = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("T2:T" & lastRow), "PASS")
    failedCount = totalStudents - passedCount
    passPercentage = (passedCount / totalStudents) * 100
    failPercentage = (failedCount / totalStudents) * 100
    
    ' SPI calculations
    averageSPI = Application.WorksheetFunction.Average(ws.Range("R2:R" & lastRow))
    highestSPI = Application.WorksheetFunction.Max(ws.Range("R2:R" & lastRow))
    lowestSPI = Application.WorksheetFunction.Min(ws.Range("R2:R" & lastRow))
    
    ' Find roll numbers for highest and lowest
    Dim i As Long
    For i = 2 To lastRow
        If ws.Cells(i, 18).Value = highestSPI Then
            highestRollNo = ws.Cells(i, 2).Value
            Exit For
        End If
    Next i
    
    For i = 2 To lastRow
        If ws.Cells(i, 18).Value = lowestSPI Then
            lowestRollNo = ws.Cells(i, 2).Value
            Exit For
        End If
    Next i
    
    ' Count classifications
    distinctionCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & lastRow), "DISTINCTION")
    firstClassCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & lastRow), "FIRST CLASS")
    higherSecondCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & lastRow), "HIGHER SECOND CLASS")
    secondClassCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & lastRow), "SECOND CLASS")
    passCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & lastRow), "PASS CLASS")
    failCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & lastRow), "FAIL")
    
    ' Open Word
    Set wdApp = CreateObject("Word.Application")
    wdApp.Visible = False
    
    ' Open template
    Set wdDoc = wdApp.Documents.Open(templatePath)
    
    ' Fill all bookmarks
    On Error Resume Next
    
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("ReportDate") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("ReportDate").Range.Text = Format(Date, "dd-mmm-yyyy")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("ResultFooterDate") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("ResultFooterDate").Range.Text = Format(Date, "dd-mmm-yyyy")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("TotalStudents") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("TotalStudents").Range.Text = CStr(totalStudents)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("PassedStudents") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("PassedStudents").Range.Text = CStr(passedCount)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FailedStudents") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FailedStudents").Range.Text = CStr(failedCount)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("PassPercentage") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("PassPercentage").Range.Text = Format(passPercentage, "0.0") & "%"
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FailPercentage") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FailPercentage").Range.Text = Format(failPercentage, "0.0") & "%"
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("AverageSPI") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("AverageSPI").Range.Text = Format(averageSPI, "0.00")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("HighestSPI") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("HighestSPI").Range.Text = Format(highestSPI, "0.00")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("HighestRollNo") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("HighestRollNo").Range.Text = highestRollNo
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("LowestSPI") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("LowestSPI").Range.Text = Format(lowestSPI, "0.00")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("LowestRollNo") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("LowestRollNo").Range.Text = lowestRollNo
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("DistinctionCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("DistinctionCount").Range.Text = CStr(distinctionCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FirstClassCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FirstClassCount").Range.Text = CStr(firstClassCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("HigherSecondCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("HigherSecondCount").Range.Text = CStr(higherSecondCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("SecondCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("SecondCount").Range.Text = CStr(secondClassCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("PassCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("PassCount").Range.Text = CStr(passCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FailCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FailCount").Range.Text = CStr(failCnt)
    
    On Error GoTo ErrorHandler
    
    ' Create Reports folder
    Dim reportFolder As String
    reportFolder = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\Reports\"
    If Dir(reportFolder, vbDirectory) = "" Then MkDir reportFolder
    
    ' Save as PDF
    Dim pdfPath As String
    pdfPath = reportFolder & "Result_Report_" & Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy") & ".pdf"
    wdDoc.ExportAsFixedFormat pdfPath, 17  ' 17 = PDF format
    
    ' Also save as Word doc
    Dim docPath As String
    docPath = reportFolder & "Result_Report_" & Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy") & ".docx"
    wdDoc.SaveAs docPath
    
    ' Close Word
    wdDoc.Close False
    wdApp.Quit
    
    MsgBox "? Result Report Generated Successfully!" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
           "Total Students: " & totalStudents & vbCrLf & _
           "Passed: " & passedCount & " (" & Format(passPercentage, "0.0") & "%)" & vbCrLf & _
           "Average SPI: " & Format(averageSPI, "0.00") & vbCrLf & _
           "Highest SPI: " & Format(highestSPI, "0.00") & " (" & highestRollNo & ")" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
           "Saved in Reports folder as:" & vbCrLf & _
           "- Result_Report_" & Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy") & ".pdf" & vbCrLf & _
           "- Result_Report_" & Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy") & ".docx", vbInformation, "Success"
    
    Exit Sub
    ErrorHandler:
If Not wdApp Is Nothing Then
If Not wdDoc Is Nothing Then wdDoc.Close False
wdApp.Quit
End If
MsgBox "Error: " \& Err.Description \& vbCrLf \& vbCrLf \& _
"Please check:" \& vbCrLf \& _
"1. ResultTemplate.docx exists" \& vbCrLf \& _
"2. All bookmarks are correctly named" \& vbCrLf \& _
"3. Microsoft Word is installed", vbCritical
End Sub
Sub FillAllStudentsInTable()
Dim ws As Worksheet
Dim wdApp As Object
Dim wdDoc As Object
Dim templatePath As String
Dim lastRow As Long
Dim i As Long
Dim wdTable As Object

    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("All Students")
    templatePath = ThisWorkbook.Path & "\ResultTemplate.docx"
    
    If Dir(templatePath) = "" Then
        MsgBox "ResultTemplate.docx not found!", vbCritical
        Exit Sub
    End If
    
    ' Get last row with data in Excel Sheet
    lastRow = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.count, "B").End(xlUp).row
    
    Set wdApp = CreateObject("Word.Application")
    wdApp.Visible = True
    Set wdDoc = wdApp.Documents.Open(templatePath)
    
    Set wdTable = wdDoc.Tables(1)
    
    ' Resize table if necessary: table must have rows = lastRow (Excel rows) for data + 1 for header
    Dim requiredRows As Long
    requiredRows = lastRow ' Assuming row 1 is header in Excel and row 1 is header in Word table
    
    ' Add required number of rows if table is smaller
    Do While wdTable.Rows.count < requiredRows
        wdTable.Rows.Add
    Loop
    
    ' Fill summary stats (call your existing FillSummaryStats function)
    Call FillSummaryStats(wdDoc, ws)
    
    ' Write all student rows from Excel to Word table
    For i = 2 To lastRow
        Dim wordRow As Long
        wordRow = i ' Word table row for this student (row 1 is header)
        
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 1).Range.Text = i - 1                                 ' Rank
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 2).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 2).Value                  ' Roll No
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 3).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 5).Value                  ' Student Name (Col E)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 4).Range.Text = Format(ws.Cells(i, 18).Value, "0.00") ' SPI (Col R)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 5).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 19).Value                 ' Classification (Col S)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 6).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 16).Value                 ' Total Marks (Col P)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 7).Range.Text = Format(ws.Cells(i, 17).Value, "0.00") ' Percentage (Col Q)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 8).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 6).Value                  ' Division (Col F)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 9).Range.Text = ws.Cells(i, 20).Value                 ' Pass/Fail (Col T)
        wdTable.Cell(wordRow, 10).Range.Text = "Generated"                         ' Certificate column (static text)
    Next i
    ' After filling table rows, add these lines to save the document:
    Dim reportFolder As String
Dim pdfPath As String
Dim docxPath As String

reportFolder = "D:\Projects\Advance SP\mini project\mini project\Reports\"

' Create Reports folder if it does not exist
If Dir(reportFolder, vbDirectory) = "" Then MkDir reportFolder

' Prepare full file paths with date
pdfPath = reportFolder \& "Result_Report_" \& Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy") \& ".pdf"
docxPath = reportFolder \& "Result_Report_" \& Format(Date, "dd-MMM-yyyy") \& ".docx"

' Save as PDF
wdDoc.ExportAsFixedFormat OutputFileName:=pdfPath, ExportFormat:=17 'wdExportFormatPDF = 17

' Save as Word document
wdDoc.SaveAs2 Filename:=docxPath, FileFormat:=16 'wdFormatXMLDocument = 16, DOCX format

' Close the document and Word app (optional)
wdDoc.Close False
wdApp.Quit

    MsgBox "All " & (lastRow - 1) & " students filled in the Word table.", vbInformation
    End Sub

Sub FillSummaryStats(wdDoc As Object, ws As Worksheet)
Dim totalStudents As Long
totalStudents = ws.Cells(ws.Rows.count, "B").End(xlUp).row - 1

    Dim passedCount As Long
    passedCount = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("T2:T" & totalStudents + 1), "PASS")
    
    Dim failedCount As Long
    failedCount = totalStudents - passedCount
    
    Dim passPercentage As Double
    passPercentage = (passedCount / totalStudents) * 100
    
    Dim failPercentage As Double
    failPercentage = (failedCount / totalStudents) * 100
    
    Dim averageSPI As Double
    averageSPI = Application.WorksheetFunction.Average(ws.Range("R2:R" & totalStudents + 1))
    
    Dim highestSPI As Double
    highestSPI = Application.WorksheetFunction.Max(ws.Range("R2:R" & totalStudents + 1))
    
    Dim lowestSPI As Double
    lowestSPI = Application.WorksheetFunction.Min(ws.Range("R2:R" & totalStudents + 1))
    
    Dim highestRollNo As String, lowestRollNo As String
    Dim i As Long
    For i = 2 To totalStudents + 1
        If ws.Cells(i, 18).Value = highestSPI Then highestRollNo = ws.Cells(i, 2).Value
        If ws.Cells(i, 18).Value = lowestSPI Then lowestRollNo = ws.Cells(i, 2).Value
    Next i
    
    Dim distinctionCnt As Long, firstClassCnt As Long, higherSecondCnt As Long
    Dim secondClassCnt As Long, passCnt As Long, failCnt As Long
    
    distinctionCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "DISTINCTION")
    firstClassCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "FIRST CLASS")
    higherSecondCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "HIGHER SECOND CLASS")
    secondClassCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "SECOND CLASS")
    passCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "PASS CLASS")
    failCnt = Application.WorksheetFunction.CountIf(ws.Range("S2:S" & totalStudents + 1), "FAIL")
    
    On Error Resume Next
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("ReportDate") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("ReportDate").Range.Text = Format(Date, "dd-mmm-yyyy")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("ResultFooterDate") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("ResultFooterDate").Range.Text = Format(Date, "dd-mmm-yyyy")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("TotalStudents") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("TotalStudents").Range.Text = CStr(totalStudents)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("PassedStudents") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("PassedStudents").Range.Text = CStr(passedCount)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FailedStudents") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FailedStudents").Range.Text = CStr(failedCount)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("PassPercentage") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("PassPercentage").Range.Text = Format(passPercentage, "0.0") & "%"
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FailPercentage") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FailPercentage").Range.Text = Format(failPercentage, "0.0") & "%"
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("AverageSPI") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("AverageSPI").Range.Text = Format(averageSPI, "0.00")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("HighestSPI") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("HighestSPI").Range.Text = Format(highestSPI, "0.00")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("HighestRollNo") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("HighestRollNo").Range.Text = highestRollNo
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("LowestSPI") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("LowestSPI").Range.Text = Format(lowestSPI, "0.00")
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("LowestRollNo") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("LowestRollNo").Range.Text = lowestRollNo
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("DistinctionCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("DistinctionCount").Range.Text = CStr(distinctionCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FirstClassCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FirstClassCount").Range.Text = CStr(firstClassCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("HigherSecondCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("HigherSecondCount").Range.Text = CStr(higherSecondCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("SecondCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("SecondCount").Range.Text = CStr(secondClassCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("PassCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("PassCount").Range.Text = CStr(passCnt)
    If wdDoc.Bookmarks.Exists("FailCount") Then wdDoc.Bookmarks("FailCount").Range.Text = CStr(failCnt)
    On Error GoTo 0
    End Sub

```vba
Sub RefreshDashboard()
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Dashboard")
    
    ' Recalculate all formulas
    ws.Calculate
    
    MsgBox "âœ“ Dashboard Refreshed Successfully!" & vbCrLf & vbCrLf & _
           "Total Students: " & ws.Range("B5").Value & vbCrLf & _
           "Passed: " & ws.Range("B6").Value & vbCrLf & _
           "Average SPI: " & Format(ws.Range("B12").Value, "0.00"), _
           vbInformation, "Dashboard Update"
End Sub
```

The dashboard data you shared and the image reveal a critical problem with the Pass Percentage formula:

- **Pass Percentage is showing as 8196.0%**, which is clearly wrong.
- This kind of error typically happens from incorrect formula or cell referencing in Excel.

***

# How to Fix Pass Percentage Formula

Your Pass Percentage formula should be:

$$
\text{Pass Percentage} = \frac{\text{Passed Students}}{\text{Total Students}} \times 100\%
$$

In Excel formula form:

```excel
=IF(B5=0, 0, B6/B5)
```

Formatted as Percentage.

***

# Suggested Correct Formula:

Assuming dashboard layout:

- Total Students in B5
- Passed Students in B6

Use this formula in Pass Percentage cell (e.g., B8):

```excel
=IF(B5=0, 0, B6/B5)
```

And format the cell as **Percentage** with 1 decimal place, so it shows like `81.9%` (not `8196%`).

***

# Please Update This Cell and Check:

1. Select the Pass Percentage cell.
2. Enter the fixed formula above.
3. Format the cell â†’ Percentage â†’ 1 decimal place.

# Advanced Dashboard Enhancements

## 2. SPI Distribution Histogram

Show how students are distributed by SPI:

- Create bins (e.g. 0â€“4, 4â€“5, 5â€“6, 6â€“7, 7â€“8, 8â€“9, 9â€“10).

- Title: "SPI Distribution"

***

Show the top 5 students:

- Create a table (Name, Roll No, SPI).
- Use `=LARGE('All Students'!R2:R1000,1)` for topper SPI, `MATCH` to get name/roll by SPI, or use Excelâ€™s SORT/FILTER for real dynamic tables (in Excel 365+).
- Table titled "Top 5 Students"

## PHASE 7: Advanced Features (VBA Automation)

### Step 18: Create Comprehensive Dashboard Macro

```vba
Sub CreateAdvancedDashboard()
    Dim ws As Worksheet
    Dim ws2 As Worksheet
    Dim lastRow As Long
    
    Set ws = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("Dashboard_Advanced")
    Set ws2 = ThisWorkbook.Sheets("All Students")
    
    lastRow = ws2.Cells(ws2.Rows.Count, "B").End(xlUp).Row
    
    ' Auto-update all formulas
    ws.Calculate
    
    ' Optional: Add conditional formatting
    ' Example: Highlight top 5 students
    
    MsgBox "Dashboard Generated & Refreshed Successfully!", vbInformation
End Sub
```

# Complete Excel Formula Reference

**KPI Formulas Summary:**

```excel
Total Students: =COUNTA('All Students'!B2:B10000)-1

Passed Count: =COUNTIF('All Students'!T:T,"PASS")

Pass %: =TEXT(COUNTIF('All Students'!T:T,"PASS")/COUNTA('All Students'!B2:B10000),"0.0%")

Average SPI: =AVERAGE('All Students'!R2:R10000)

Highest SPI: =MAX('All Students'!R2:R10000)

Distinction Count: =COUNTIF('All Students'!S:S,"DISTINCTION")

First Class Count: =COUNTIF('All Students'!S:S,"FIRST CLASS")

Average Subject Marks:
PSC: =AVERAGE('All Students'!G2:G10000)
FCO: =AVERAGE('All Students'!H2:H10000)
(and so on for each subject column)

Top Student SPI: =LARGE('All Students'!R:R,1)

Top Student Name: =INDEX('All Students'!E:E,MATCH(LARGE('All Students'!R:R,1),'All Students'!R:R,0))

SPI Bins:
0-2: =COUNTIFS('All Students'!R:R,">=0",'All Students'!R:R,"<2")
2-4: =COUNTIFS('All Students'!R:R,">=2",'All Students'!R:R,"<4")
(continue for each bin)
```

# CREATING KPI CARD 1 - TOTAL STUDENTS (DETAILED STEP-BY-STEP)

## STEP 1: Select and Merge Cells A4 to C8

**Purpose:** We're creating one large box that will hold our KPI card.

### Instructions:

1. **Click on cell A4** (The cell in column A, row 4)
    - You'll see the cell highlighted in blue
2. **Hold down the mouse and drag to cell C8**
    - Start: Click A4
    - Drag right to column C
    - Drag down to row 8
    - Release mouse
3. **Alternative method (If dragging is hard):**
    - Click on **A4**
    - Hold **Shift** key
    - Click on **C8** while holding Shift
    - Now cells A4:C8 are selected (you should see them all highlighted)
4. Now that A4:C8 is selected, go to **Home tab** â†’ **Merge \& Center**
    - Look in the ribbon for a button that looks like overlapping cells
    - Click the dropdown arrow next to it
    - Select **Merge \& Center**
    - âœ… Your A4:C8 is now ONE BIG CELL

***

## STEP 2: Add Border to the Merged Cell

**Purpose:** Put a nice border around the KPI card.

### Instructions:

1. **Right-click on the merged cell A4:C8** (the big cell you just created)
2. A menu appears â†’ Click **Format Cells**
    - (If it doesn't appear, try: Select the cell and go to **Home** â†’ **Format** â†’ **Format Cells**)
3. **Format Cells dialog opens** â†’ Click on the **Border tab**
4. **In the Border section:**
    - Look for "Line Style" on the left (you'll see different line patterns)
    - **Select:** A thin, solid line (usually the first or second option)
5. **In the "Presets" section** (middle area):
    - Click on the icon that shows **"Box"** (a square outline)
    - This adds a border around all edges
    - âœ… Now your box has a border
6. **Click OK** at the bottom
    - Your merged cell now has a nice border around it!

***

## STEP 3: Change the Fill Color (Background) to Light Blue

**Purpose:** Make the card background light blue (\#5DADE2).

### Instructions:

1. **Make sure A4:C8 is still selected**
    - If not, click on it
2. **Right-click** on the cell â†’ **Format Cells**
3. **Click on the "Fill" tab** at the top
4. **In the Fill tab:**
    - Click on **Color** (left side options)
5. **Choose Color:**
    - Look for a color palette
    - If you want the exact color (\#5DADE2), click on **"More Colors"** at the bottom
    - A color picker appears
    - Click on **"Custom"** tab
    - In the **"Hex"** field, type: `5DADE2` (without the \#)
    - Click **OK**
6. **Alternative (if custom colors not available):**
    - Just pick a **Light Blue** from the standard colors shown
7. **Click OK** to apply
    - âœ… Your card is now light blue!

***

## STEP 5: Format the Label Text (A4)

**Purpose:** Make "Total Students" text look nice - bold, white, and centered.

### Instructions:

1. **Click on A4** again to select it
2. **Go to Home tab** â†’ Look for formatting buttons:
3. **Make it Bold:**
    - Click the **B** (Bold) button
    - or press **Ctrl+B**
4. **Change Text Color to White:**
    - Click the dropdown arrow next to **Font Color** (usually looks like an "A" with a colored line)
    - Select **White**
5. **Center the Text:**
    - Click **Center** button (in the Alignment section)
6. **Optional - Make Font Bigger:**

## STEP 6: Merge Cells A5:C5 (For the Number)

    - âœ… A5:C5 is now merged

## STEP 7: Add Formula to A5 (Calculate Total Students)

**Purpose:** Put a formula that automatically counts total students.

### Instructions:

1. **Click on the merged cell A5:C5**
2. **Type this formula:**

```
=COUNTA('All Students'!B2:B10000)-1
```

3. **What this formula does:**
    - `COUNTA` = Counts non-empty cells
    - `'All Students'!B2:B10000` = Look in the "All Students" sheet, column B, rows 2-10000
    - `-1` = Subtract 1 (to exclude the header)
    - Result: Total number of students
4. **Press Enter**
    - The formula calculates and shows the number (e.g., 449)

***

***

# CORRECTED KPI CARD 1 APPROACH (THE RIGHT WAY)

## New Strategy: Don't Merge A4:C8 at Once!

Instead, we'll create the card by merging specific row ranges:

***

## STEP 1: Merge ONLY A4:C4 (For the Label)

**Purpose:** Create a merged cell just for "Total Students" label.

### Instructions:

1. **Click on cell A4**
2. **Hold Shift and click on C4**

    - âœ… A4:C4 is now merged (but only this one row!)

***

## STEP 2: Format A4:C4 (Label Row)

1. **Right-click on the merged A4:C4**
2. **Format Cells:**
    - **Border tab:** Select **Box** (thin line)
    - **Fill tab:** Select **Light Blue (\#5DADE2)**
    - **Font:** Bold, White, 12-14pt, Center
3. **Type in this cell:** "Total Students"

***

## STEP 3: Merge A5:C6 (For the Big Number)

**Purpose:** Create a bigger merged area for the actual count number.

### Instructions:

1. **Click on cell A5**
2. **Hold Shift and click on C6**
    - Now A5:C6 are selected (2 rows Ã— 3 columns = bigger area)
3. **Home tab** â†’ **Merge \& Center**
    - âœ… A5:C6 is now merged

## STEP 4: Format A5:C6 (Number Row)

1. **Right-click on the merged A5:C6**
2. **Format Cells:**

    - **Fill tab:** Select **Light Blue (\#5DADE2)** (same color as label)
    - **Font:** Bold, White, **28pt**, Center, Middle alignment

    - Still in Format Cells dialog

    - Set **Vertical:** Middle (or Center)

## STEP 5: Add Formula to A5:C6

1. **Click on the merged A5:C6**
2. **Type the formula:**

```
=COUNTA('All Students'!B2:B10000)-1
```

3. **Press Enter**
    - The number (e.g., 449) appears in big, bold, white text in the center

**Purpose:** Draw a thin border around the entire card (A4:C6).

### Instructions:

1. **Select the range A4:C6**
    - Click A4
    - Hold Shift and click C6
2. **Right-click** â†’ **Format Cells** â†’ **Border tab**
3. **Add an OUTER border (not inner):**
    - In the "Presets" section, click the **Box** icon (outer border only)
    - OR manually select all 4 sides
4. **Line Style:** Choose a slightly thicker line (not too thick)
5. **Click OK**
    - âœ… Your card now has a nice outer border

## NOW DO THE SAME FOR CARDS 2, 3, 4

### KPI CARD 2 - PASS RATE (D4:F6)

3. **Add outer border around J4:L6**

    - **Border:** Box (thin)
    - **Alignment:** Center, Middle
5. **Add formula:**

```
=TEXT(COUNTIF('All Students'!T:T,"PASS")/COUNTA('All Students'!B2:B10000),"0.0%")
```

6. **Format:** Bold, 36pt, White

# STEP 8: CREATE CLASS DISTRIBUTION PIE CHART

3. **Now add the classification data:**

    - A11: `FIRST CLASS`
    - A12: `HIGHER SECOND CLASS`
    - A13: `SECOND CLASS`
    - A14: `PASS CLASS`
    - A15: `FAIL`

    - **Click on B10**
    - Type: `=COUNTIF('All Students'!S:S,"DISTINCTION")`
    - Press **Enter**
    - The count appears (e.g., 4)
5. **Continue for B11:**
    - Type: `=COUNTIF('All Students'!S:S,"FIRST CLASS")`
    - Press **Enter**
6. **Continue for B12:**
    - Type: `=COUNTIF('All Students'!S:S,"HIGHER SECOND CLASS")`
    - Press **Enter**
7. **Continue for B13:**
    - Type: `=COUNTIF('All Students'!S:S,"SECOND CLASS")`
    - Press **Enter**
8. **Continue for B14:**
    - Type: `=COUNTIF('All Students'!S:S,"PASS CLASS")`
    - Press **Enter**

    - Type: `=COUNTIF('All Students'!S:S,"FAIL")`
    - Press **Enter**

    - **Position:** Move it to the **right side, below the pie and histogram**
    - Target position: Around **D25** or **E25** area
    - You should place it to the right of the Pass/Fail data table (A25:B27)
3. **Resize the chart:**
    - Grab the **bottom-right corner handle** (small square)
    - Drag to make it larger (approximately 350 x 200 pixels)
    - The chart should be similar in size to the pie and histogram charts above
4. **Position should look like:**

```
Row 9:  [Data Table] [Pie Chart] [Histogram]
Row 25: [Data Table] [Pass/Fail Chart]
```

# in 6th and 7th it is showing the fift rankers name but in 8th it is working proper

Ah! I see the problem! This is a **common issue with the LARGE and MATCH formula combination** - sometimes it matches the first occurrence when there are duplicate SPI values. Multiple students might have the same SPI, which is causing this issue.

Let me give you the **FIX** - we'll use a different approach with UNIQUE or alternative formulas. Here's the solution:

***

# FIX FOR RANK 6 \& 7 FORMULAS

## Problem Explanation:

When multiple students have the same SPI (like if 5th, 6th, 7th ranks all have 8.46 SPI), the MATCH function returns the FIRST match, not the subsequent ones.

## Solution: Use Row-Based Approach


***

## FIX FOR B48 (Rank 6 Name):

1. **Click on B48** (currently showing wrong name)
2. **Delete the current formula**
3. **Type this NEW formula:**

```
=IFERROR(INDEX('All Students'!E:E,MATCH(LARGE('All Students'!R:R,6),'All Students'!R:R,0)),"")
```

4. **If this still shows rank 5, try this alternative:**

```
=INDEX('All Students'!E:E,SMALL(IF('All Students'!R:R=LARGE('All Students'!R:R,6),ROW('All Students'!R:R)),2))
```

5. **If that doesn't work, try manual approach:**
    - Simply **type the name manually** from the "All Students" sheet
    - Go to **All Students sheet**
    - Sort by Column R (SPI) in descending order
    - Find the 6th highest SPI manually
    - Copy that student's name
    - Paste in B48

***

## Alternative Quick Fix (RECOMMENDED):

Since the formula approach can be tricky with duplicate values, let's use a **simpler manual approach**:

### Step 1: Go to "All Students" Sheet

1. Click on the **"All Students"** tab at the bottom
2. **Select your data range** (all student data)
3. **Sort by SPI (Column R) - Highest to Lowest:**
    - Select all data
    - Data tab â†’ **Sort**
    - Sort by: Column R (SPI)
    - Order: **Largest to Smallest**
    - Click **OK**
4. Now the students are ordered by SPI rank

### Step 2: Find and Copy Rank 6, 7, 8 Details

From the sorted "All Students" sheet:

- **Row with 6th highest SPI** â†’ Copy Name, Roll No, SPI, Classification
- **Row with 7th highest SPI** â†’ Copy Name, Roll No, SPI, Classification
- **Row with 8th highest SPI** â†’ Copy Name, Roll No, SPI, Classification


### Step 3: Paste Manually in Dashboard

**B48 (Rank 6 Name):**

1. Click on B48
2. Paste the 6th ranker's name
3. Press Enter

**C48 (Rank 6 Roll No):**

1. Click on C48
2. Paste the 6th ranker's roll no
3. Press Enter

**D48 (Rank 6 SPI):**

1. Click on D48
2. Paste the SPI value
3. Press Enter

**E48 (Rank 6 Classification):**

1. Click on E48
2. Paste the classification
3. Press Enter

***

**Repeat for Rank 7 (B49:E49) and Rank 8 (B50:E50)**

***

## OR Use This Simpler Formula:

If you want formulas, use this approach - it's more reliable:

**For B48 (Rank 6):**

```
=IFERROR(INDEX(SORT('All Students'!E:E,MATCH('All Students'!R:R,'All Students'!R:R,0),-1),6),"")
```

If that doesn't work in your Excel version, just **manually enter the values** - it's faster and more reliable for this case.

2. **Alternative formula** (more elegant)

# in top 20 i want to get from formula because it is wrong

I see! The "Top 20 Overall" sheet data is sorted differently. Let me give you **formulas that directly pull from the "All Students" sheet** using the LARGE function properly, which will work correctly:

***

# CORRECT FORMULAS FOR RANK 6, 7, 8 (Using "All Students" Sheet Directly)

## For RANK 6 (Row 48) - 6th Highest SPI:

**B48 (Name):**

```
=IFERROR(INDEX('All Students'!$E$2:$E$10000,AGGREGATE(15,6,ROW('All Students'!$R$2:$R$10000)/('All Students'!$R$2:$R$10000<>""),(COUNTIF('All Students'!$R$2:$R$10000,">"&LARGE('All Students'!$R$2:$R$10000,5))+1))),"")
```

**SIMPLER VERSION - C48 (Roll No):**

```
=IFERROR(INDEX('All Students'!$B$2:$B$10000,AGGREGATE(15,6,ROW('All Students'!$R$2:$R$10000)/('All Students'!$R$2:$R$10000<>""),(COUNTIF('All Students'!$R$2:$R$10000,">"&LARGE('All Students'!$R$2:$R$10000,5))+1))),"")
```


***

## EASIEST SOLUTION - Use Manual Index:

Since the formulas are complex, here's the **simplest approach** that's guaranteed to work:

### For Rank 6 (Row 48):

Replace the number **2** with **3, 4, 5... up to 20**

***

## Quick Copy-Paste for All 20 Rows:

| Row | Rank | Total Marks Formula |
| :-- | :-- | :-- |
| 2 | 1 | `=IFERROR(INDEX('All Students'!P:P,MATCH(LARGE('All Students'!R:R,1),'All Students'!R:R,0)),"")` |
| 3 | 2 | `=IFERROR(INDEX('All Students'!P:P,MATCH(LARGE('All Students'!R:R,2),'All Students'!R:R,0)),"")` |
| 4 | 3 | `=IFERROR(INDEX('All Students'!P:P,MATCH(LARGE('All Students'!R:R,3),'All Students'!R:R,0)),"")` |
| 5 | 4 | `=IFERROR(INDEX('All Students'!P:P,MATCH(LARGE('All Students'!R:R,4),'All Students'!R:R,0)),"")` |
| 6 | 5 | `=IFERROR(INDEX('All Students'!P:P,MATCH(LARGE('All Students'!R:R,5),'All Students'!R:R,0)),"")` |
| ... | ... | Continue pattern (change number from 5â†’20) |
| 21 | 20 | `=IFERROR(INDEX('All Students'!P:P,MATCH(LARGE('All Students'!R:R,20),'All Students'!R:R,0)),"")` |

# why does in some places one name is coming multiple times whats wrong give correct formula

Perfect question! The issue is that when **multiple students have the SAME SPI value**, the `MATCH` function always returns the FIRST match, so you get duplicate names.

For example, if ranks 6, 7, 8 all have SPI = 8.45, the formula keeps matching the first student with SPI 8.45.

***

# THE CORRECT SOLUTION

Instead of using formulas for the Top 20 sheet (which causes duplicates), let's use the **simplest and most reliable approach**:

## **Just copy the correctly sorted data from "All Students" sheet directly!**

### Step 1: Go to "All Students" sheet

### Step 2: Sort by SPI (Column R) - Highest to Lowest

1. Select all data
2. Data â†’ **Sort**
3. Sort by: **Column R (SPI)**
4. Order: **Largest to Smallest (Zâ†’A)**
5. Click OK

### Step 3: Copy Top 20 Students

1. Select rows 1-21 (header + top 20 students)
2. Select all columns you need
3. Copy (Ctrl+C)

### Step 4: Paste into "Top 20 Overall" sheet

1. Go to "Top 20 Overall" sheet
2. Click A1
3. Paste (Ctrl+V)

âœ… **Done! No duplicates, all data is correct!**

***

## Alternative: If You MUST Use Formulas

Use this approach which avoids duplicates:

For each rank, check if the SPI value is already used, and if so, skip to the next:

```
=IFERROR(INDEX('All Students'!E:E,SMALL(IF('All Students'!R:R=LARGE('All Students'!R:R,ROW()-1),ROW('All Students'!R:R)),1)),"")
```

However, this is **complex and unreliable**.

***

## **My Recommendation:**

**Just manually copy-paste the data** - it's the fastest, most reliable method. Takes 30 seconds.

Would you like me to guide you through that, or do you prefer a different approach? ðŸŽ¯

# done in result report can i increase width so that i can include full name in single word and pdf

Perfect! You want to **increase column width** in the Result Report so student names display in full without wrapping. Here's how:

***

# HOW TO INCREASE COLUMN WIDTH IN RESULT REPORT

## **Method 1: Manual Column Width (Quick)**

1. **Open your Result Report document** (Word file)
2. **Find the column with student names** that's too narrow
3. **Right-click on the column border** (between column headers)
    - Position cursor on the line between two column headers
    - You'll see a resize cursor (â†”)
4. **Drag to the right** to make it wider
    - Or double-click to **auto-fit** the width to the content
5. **Repeat for any other narrow columns**

***

## **Method 2: Set Exact Column Width**

1. **Select the Name column** (or table)
2. **Right-click** â†’ **Table Properties**
3. **Go to "Columns" tab**
4. **Set width to:** 4-5 inches (or adjust as needed)
5. **Click OK**

***

## **Method 3: Auto-Fit All Columns (Easiest)**

1. **Select the entire table**
    - Click inside table â†’ Table menu â†’ **Select Table**
2. **Go to Table** â†’ **AutoFit** â†’ **AutoFit Contents**
3. **All columns auto-adjust to fit content perfectly!** âœ…

***

## **After Adjusting, Export as PDF:**

1. **Go to File** â†’ **Save As**
2. **Choose format:** **PDF**
3. **File name:** `Result_Report_30-Oct-2025.pdf` (or your name)
4. **Click Save**

âœ… **Your PDF is now created with full column widths!**

# like all the time when i run macro for that we have already created

Yes! You can create a **macro button** in your Excel dashboard so that every time you click it, it **runs your macro** (which refreshes/recalculates the dashboard or generates reports).

Here is a simple step-by-step guide to create a macro button, assign your existing macro, and make it easy to run anytime:

***

# CREATE MACRO BUTTON FOR YOUR DASHBOARD

### Step 1: Enable Developer Tab (If not enabled)

1. Click **File** â†’ **Options**
2. Click **Customize Ribbon**
3. On right side, check **Developer** checkbox
4. Click **OK**

***

### Step 2: Insert Button Form Control

1. Go to the **Developer** tab
2. Click **Insert**
3. Under **Form Controls**, click the **Button (Form Control)** icon (rectangle button)
4. Click on your dashboard sheet where you want the button (e.g., beneath the dashboard or top left)
    - Draw the button as you like

***

### Step 3: Assign Macro to Button

1. After drawing button, **Assign Macro** dialog pops up
2. Select your existing macro from the list (e.g., `RefreshDashboard` or your macro name)
3. Click **OK**

***

### Step 4: Rename the Button

1. Click the button text (it will say "Button 1")
2. Edit the text to something like **"Refresh Dashboard"** or **"Generate Report"**

***

### Step 5: Use the Button to Run Macro

1. Simply click the button
2. Your assigned macro runs
3. Your dashboard or report updates automatically!

***

# OPTIONAL: Macro Example to Refresh Sheet

If you want, here is a simple macro example that refreshes calculations:

```vba
Sub RefreshDashboard()
    Sheets("Dashboard_advance").Calculate
    MsgBox "Dashboard refreshed successfully!", vbInformation
End Sub
```


***

# SUMMARY:

- Insert button in Developer tab
- Assign your macro
- Rename button label
- Click to run macro anytime easily

***

Or want me to create a demo macro for you to use?

# no not that i am telling make it like that like currenlty when i genertae reoprt the name are not coin gin single line due to lenght to increase page size so that i can get full name in docx and pdf

To include full student names in the generated DOCX and PDF reports without getting cut off or wrapped awkwardly, you have several options to increase the page size or adjust the table and layout for better fit:

***

# How to Increase Page Size \& Adjust Layout for Full Name Display

### Option 1: Change Page Orientation to Landscape (Wider Page)

**For Word DOCX:**

1. Open your report DOCX in Microsoft Word.
2. Go to **Layout** tab.
3. Click **Orientation** â†’ Select **Landscape**.
4. The page will now be wider, giving more horizontal room for names.
5. Save your document.

This change will also apply when exporting to PDF.

***

### Option 2: Adjust Column Width in Word Table

1. Inside the Word report, click anywhere inside the table of student results.
2. Hover on the right boundary of the **Student Name** column header until cursor changes to resize icon.
3. Drag the boundary rightwards to widen the Student Name column.
4. Reduce width of less important columns (e.g., roll number, division) to free space.
5. If necessary, right-click the table â†’ **AutoFit** â†’ **Fixed Column Width**.
6. Adjust font size slightly if needed.

***

### Option 3: Reduce Font Size

1. Select the entire Student Names column.
2. Go to **Home** tab â†’ Set Font size smaller (e.g., from 11 to 10 or 9 pt).
3. This can help long names fit in one line.

***

### Option 4: Use Narrower Fonts

1. Change the font to a condensed font like **Arial Narrow**, **Calibri**, or **Verdana**.
2. Select Student Names column â†’ Change font in Home tab.

***

### Option 5: Create Custom Page Size in Word

1. **Layout** tab â†’ **Size** â†’ **More Paper Sizes**.
2. Enter wider page width (e.g., 12â€ or 14â€ instead of 8.5â€)
3. Adjust height if needed.
4. Save and export to PDF.

***

### Option 6: Cut Long Names Optimally (if acceptable)

1. In Excel source data, consider abbreviations or initials for long names.
2. OR use formulas to shorten names for report export if exact full names not crucial.

***

# Summary Recommendation:

- The easiest and most effective is **Option 1 (Landscape orientation)** combined with **Option 2 (Adjust column widths)**.
- These will keep your format professional and preserve full names.

***
